<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On July 23, 2015, Comcast Corporation (&#147;Comcast&#148;) issued a press release reporting the results of its operations for the three and six months ended June 30, 2015.&#160; The press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. Exhibit 99.2 sets forth the reasons Comcast believes that presentation of the non-GAAP financial measures contained in the press release provides useful information to investors regarding Comcast&#146;s financial condition and results of operations. To the extent material, Exhibit 99.2 also discloses the additional purposes, if any, for which Comcast&#146;s management uses these non-GAAP financial measures.&nbsp; A reconciliation of these non-GAAP financial measures with the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures is included in the press release itself.&#160; Comcast does not intend for this Item 2.02 or Exhibit 99.1 or Exhibit 99.2 to be treated as &#147;filed&#148; under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or incorporated by reference into its filings under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;">
<tr>
<td width="17%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:17.96%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="64%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:64.1%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:2.5pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="17%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:17.94%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:center;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>   </tr>
<tr>
<td width="17%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:17.96%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="64%" valign="top" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #C9C9C9 1.5pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:64.1%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="3" face="Arial" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">COMCAST REPORTS 2nd QUARTER 2015 RESULTS</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="17%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:17.94%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:center;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:4.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Consolidated 2nd Quarter 2015 Highlights:</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Consolidated Revenue Increased 11.3%, Operating Cash Flow Increased 8.0%, and Operating Income Increased 7.9%</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Free Cash Flow Increased 30.0%</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Earnings per Share Increased 10.5% to $0.84; Excluding Adjustments, EPS Increased 12.0%</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Quarterly Dividends and Quarterly Share Repurchases Increased $878 Million, or 65.8%, to $2.2 Billion</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cable Communications 2nd Quarter 2015 Highlights:</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Cable Communications Revenue Increased 6.3% and Operating Cash Flow Increased 5.1%</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Customer Relationships Increased by 31,000, a 56,000 Improvement from the Second Quarter of 2014</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Total Revenue per Customer Relationship Increased 4.5%</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Video Customer Net Losses Declined to 69,000, a 52% Improvement from the Second Quarter of 2014, and The Best Second Quarter Result in Nine Years</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">X1 Deployments Continue to Accelerate; Nearly One-Third of Triple Play Customers Now Have X1</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">High-Speed Internet Customers Increased by 180,000 and Revenue Grew 10.0%</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Business Services Revenue Increased 20.4%; Second Largest Contributor to Cable Revenue Growth for 17 of the Last 18 Quarters</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NBCUniversal 2nd Quarter 2015 Highlights:</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">NBCUniversal Revenue Increased 20.2% and Operating Cash Flow Increased 19.4%</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">NBC Ended the Broadcast Season Ranked #1 Among Adults 18-49 for the Second Year in a Row</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Universal Pictures is #1 in Domestic and International Box Office Receipts This Year</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Filmed Entertainment Revenue Increased 92.7% and Operating Cash Flow More Than Doubled</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font face="Arial">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Arial">Theme Parks Revenue Increased 25.7% and Operating Cash Flow Increased 44.9%</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">PHILADELPHIA &#150; July&nbsp;23, 2015&#133; Comcast Corporation (NASDAQ: CMCSA, CMCSK) today reported results for the quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:6.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Brian L. Roberts, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of Comcast Corporation, said, &#147;Our second quarter results, including 11.3% revenue growth and 8.0% operating cash flow growth, demonstrate the strength and momentum we are seeing across our businesses.&#160; In Cable, high-speed Internet and business services continued to perform extremely well, and, significantly, this was the best second quarter video customer results we&#146;ve had in nine years. Our focus on accelerating the deployment of our transformative X1 platform, as well as efforts to improve customer service, are clearly making a difference, with lower churn across all product categories. NBCUniversal had an exceptional quarter, led by the record-breaking box office performances of <i>Jurassic World</i> and <i>Furious 7</i> and continued strong momentum in our theme parks. In addition, NBC won the 2014-2015 broadcast season for adults 18-49. Our teams are executing incredibly well across our strong and diversified portfolio, and I am excited for what we can deliver in the rest of 2015 and beyond.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.0pt;">For additional detail on segment revenue and expenses, customer metrics, capital expenditures, and free cash flow, please refer to the trending schedules on Comcast&#146;s Investor Relations website at www.cmcsa.com or www.cmcsk.com.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Consolidated Revenue</font></i></b><font face="Arial"> for the second quarter of 2015 increased 11.3% to $18.7 billion.<b><i style="font-weight:bold;"> Consolidated Operating Cash Flow</i></b> increased 8.0% to $6.3 billion. Excluding $79 million of Time Warner Cable and Charter transaction-related costs in the second quarter of 2015 and $44 million in the second quarter of 2014, consolidated operating cash flow increased 8.5% (See Table 5). <b><i style="font-weight:bold;">Consolidated Operating Income</i></b> increased 7.9% to $4.1 billion.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, consolidated revenue increased 6.8% to $36.6 billion.&#160; Consolidated operating cash flow increased 7.8% to $12.2 billion.&#160; Excluding $178 million of transaction-related costs in the first six months of 2015 and $61 million in the first six months of 2014, consolidated operating cash flow increased 8.7% (See Table 5). Consolidated operating income increased 8.4% to $8.0 billion.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Earnings per Share (EPS)</font></i></b><font face="Arial"> for the second quarter of 2015 was $0.84, a 10.5% increase from the $0.76 reported in the second quarter of 2014. Excluding a gain on the settlement of a contingent consideration liability with General Electric Company, a gain on the sale of an investment, a loss resulting from the early redemption of debt, transaction-related costs, and a loss on an investment in the second quarter of 2015, as well as a gain on the sale of an investment and transaction-related costs in the second quarter of 2014, EPS increased 12.0% to $0.84 (See Table 4).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EPS for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 was $1.65, a 12.2% increase from the $1.47 reported in the prior year.&#160; Excluding a gain on the settlement of a contingent consideration liability with General Electric Company, gains on the sale of an investment and business, a loss resulting from the early redemption of debt, transaction-related costs, and a loss on an investment in the first six months of 2015, as well as gains on the sales of investments, a favorable resolution of a prior acquisition contingency and transaction-related costs in the first six months of 2014, EPS increased 14.0% to $1.63 (See Table 4).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Capital Expenditures</font></i></b><font face="Arial"> increased 9.6% to $2.0 billion in the second quarter of 2015 compared to the second quarter of 2014. Cable Communications&#146; capital expenditures increased 12.3% to $1.7 billion in the second quarter of 2015, primarily reflecting increased spending on customer premise equipment related to the deployment of the X1 platform and wireless gateways, our ongoing investment in network infrastructure to increase network capacity, and increased investment in support capital as we expand our cloud based initiatives. Cable capital expenditures represented 14.3% of Cable revenue in the second quarter of 2015 compared to 13.5% in last year&#146;s second quarter.&#160; NBCUniversal&#146;s capital expenditures decreased 8.5% to $272 million in the second quarter of 2015, primarily reflecting decreased investments in facilities, partially offset by increased spending at our Theme Parks.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, capital expenditures increased 13.9% to $3.7 billion compared to the prior year.&#160; Cable Communications capital expenditures increased $483 million, or 18.3%, to $3.1 billion and represented 13.5% of Cable revenue compared to 12.1% in 2014.&#160; NBCUniversal&#146;s capital expenditures decreased $49 million, or 8.2%, to $540 million for the first six months of 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Free Cash Flow</font></i></b><font face="Arial"> increased 30.0% to $1.5 billion in the second quarter of 2015 compared to $1.2 billion in the second quarter of 2014, reflecting growth in consolidated operating cash flow and improvements in working capital, partially offset by higher capital expenditures and cash taxes. Free cash flow for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 increased 17.7% to $4.7 billion compared to $4.0 billion in 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Dividends and Share Repurchases. </font></i></b><font face="Arial">During the </font><font face="Arial">second</font><font face="Arial"> quarter of 201</font><font face="Arial">5</font><font face="Arial">, Comcast paid dividends totaling $</font><font face="Arial">628</font><font face="Arial"> million and repurchased </font><font face="Arial">27.4</font><font face="Arial"> million of its common shares for $</font><font face="Arial">1.6 b</font><font face="Arial">illion. </font><font face="Arial">&#160;In the first six months of 2015, Comcast has repurchased 62.5 million of its common shares for $3.6 billion. As of June&nbsp;30, 2015, Comcast had $6.4 billion available under its share repurchase authorization.</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:2.4pt 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="5%" valign="top" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:5.0%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:2.4pt 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="7%" valign="top" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:7.48%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:2.4pt 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><i><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-style:italic;">12.1%</font></i></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="top" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.48%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:2.4pt 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Revenue</font></i></b><font face="Arial"> for Cable Communications increased 6.3% to $11.7 billion in the second quarter of 2015 compared to $11.0 billion in the second quarter of 2014, driven by increases of 10.0% in high-speed Internet, 20.4% in business services and 3.7% in video. The increase in Cable revenue reflects increased customer relationships (See below), customers receiving higher levels of service and customers taking additional services, as well as rate adjustments.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, Cable revenue increased 6.3% to $23.2 billion compared to $21.8 billion in 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.0pt;">3</font><a name="PB_3_074945_7608"></a></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Customer Relationships </font></i></b><font face="Arial">increased by 31,000 to 27.3 million in the second quarter of 2015, a 56,000 improvement compared to the second quarter of 2014 and driven by increases in double and triple product relationships.&#160; </font><font face="Arial">At the end of the second quarter, our double and triple product customers increased to 69% of our total customer relationships compared to 68% in the second quarter of 2014.</font><font face="Arial"> Video net losses improved 52% year-over-year to 69,000 and were the best result for a second quarter in nine years, while H</font><font face="Arial">igh-Speed Internet customers grew by 180,000 and Voice net additions were 49,000.</font></p>

<td width="10%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:10.4%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in .05in .0001pt 0in;text-align:right;"><b><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">31</font></b></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Operating Cash Flow</font></i></b><font face="Arial"> for Cable Communications increased 5.1% to $4.8 billion in the second quarter of 2015 compared to $4.6 billion in the second quarter of 2014, reflecting higher revenue, partially offset by a 7.2% increase in operating expenses primarily related to higher video programming costs, as well as an increase in technical and product support expenses driven by an acceleration in the deployment of X1 and investments to improve the customer experience. As a result, this quarter&#146;s operating cash flow margin was 40.9% compared to 41.4% in the prior year period.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, Cable operating cash flow increased 5.7% to $9.5 billion compared to $9.0 billion in 2014.&#160; Year-to-date operating cash flow margin was 40.9% compared to 41.1% in 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.0pt;">4</font><a name="PB_4_075012_8146"></a></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Revenue </font></i></b><font face="Arial">for NBCUniversal increased 20.2% to $7.2 billion in the second quarter of 2015 compared to $6.0 billion in the second quarter of 2014. <b><i style="font-weight:bold;">Operating Cash Flow</i></b> increased 19.4% to $1.7 billion compared to $1.4 billion in the second quarter of 2014, driven by strong results at Filmed Entertainment and Theme Parks.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, NBCUniversal revenue increased 7.3% to $13.8 billion compared to $12.9 billion in 2014. Excluding $376 million of revenue generated by the broadcast of the NFL&#146;s Super Bowl in the first quarter of 2015 and $1.1 billion of revenue generated by the Sochi Olympics in the first quarter of 2014, revenue increased 14.2% (See Table 5).&#160; Operating cash flow increased 16.8% to $3.2 billion compared to $2.7 billion in the first six months of 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cable Networks</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the second quarter of 2015, revenue from the Cable Networks segment decreased 1.0% to $2.5 billion, reflecting a 26.3% decrease in content licensing and other revenue due to the timing of content provided under our licensing agreements and a 3.0% decline in advertising revenue, partially offset by a 5.6% increase in distribution revenue. Operating cash flow decreased 4.6% to $872 million compared to $914 million in the second quarter of 2014, reflecting lower revenue and modest increases in other operating and administrative expenses.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, revenue from the Cable Networks segment decreased 3.5% to $4.8 billion compared to $5.0 billion in 2014. Excluding $257 million of revenue generated by the Sochi Olympics in the first quarter of 2014, revenue increased 1.8% (See Table 5).&#160; Operating cash flow decreased 2.2% to $1.8 billion in the first six months of 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Broadcast Television</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the second quarter of 2015, revenue from the Broadcast Television segment remained flat at $1.8 billion, reflecting a slight increase in advertising revenue and higher retransmission consent fees, which were offset by lower content licensing revenue. Operating cash flow decreased 3.7% to $231 million compared to the second quarter of 2014, primarily reflecting increases in other operating and administrative expenses, which were largely offset by a decrease in programming and production costs associated with the timing of the airing of certain shows in our primetime schedule.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, revenue from the Broadcast Television segment decreased 8.5% to $4.1 billion compared to $4.4 billion in 2014.&#160; Excluding $376 million of revenue generated by the NFL&#146;s Super Bowl in the first quarter of 2015, as well as $846 million of revenue generated by the Sochi Olympics in the first quarter of 2014, revenue increased 2.6% (See Table 5).&#160; Operating cash flow increased 14.0% to $413 million compared to $362 million in the first six months of 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Filmed Entertainment</font></b></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the </font><font face="Arial">second </font><font face="Arial">quarter of 201</font><font face="Arial">5</font><font face="Arial">, revenue from the Filmed Entertainment segment increased </font><font face="Arial">92.7</font><font face="Arial">% to $</font><font face="Arial">2.3</font><font face="Arial"> billion, driven by higher </font><font face="Arial">theatrical revenue from the record performances of <i>Furious 7 </i>and<i> Jurassic World</i>.</font><font face="Arial"> Operating cash flow </font><font face="Arial">increased $227 million to $422</font><font face="Arial"> million, reflecting </font><font face="Arial">higher revenue, partially offset by an increase in the amortization of film costs and higher advertising, marketing and promotion expense due to a larger film slate.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, revenue from the Filmed Entertainment segment increased 46.9% to $3.7 billion compared to $2.5 billion in 2014.&#160; Operating cash flow increased 48.1% to $715 million compared to $483 million in the first six months of 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Theme Parks</font></b></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the </font><font face="Arial">second </font><font face="Arial">quarter of 201</font><font face="Arial">5</font><font face="Arial">, revenue from the Theme Parks segment increased </font><font face="Arial">25.7</font><font face="Arial">% to $</font><font face="Arial">773</font><font face="Arial"> million compared to</font><font face="Arial"> $615 million in </font><font face="Arial">the </font><font face="Arial">second </font><font face="Arial">quarter of 201</font><font face="Arial">4</font><font face="Arial">,</font><font face="Arial"> reflecting higher guest attendance and per capita spending, driven by the continued success of Orlando&#146;s <i>The Wizarding World of Harry Potter</i>&#153; <i>&#150; Diagon Alley</i>&#153;. Second </font><font face="Arial">quarter operating cash flow </font><font face="Arial">increased 44.9</font><font face="Arial">% to $</font><font face="Arial">354</font><font face="Arial"> million compared to </font><font face="Arial">$244 million in the same period last year, reflecting higher revenue, partially offset by an increase in operating costs to support the new attractions</font><font face="Arial" style="border:none;">.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, revenue from the Theme Parks segment increased 29.2% to $1.4 billion compared to $1.1 billion in 2014.&#160; Operating cash flow increased 48.9% to $617 million compared to $414 million in the first six months of 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.0pt;">5</font><a name="PB_5_075022_7091"></a></p>

<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Headquarters, Other and Eliminations</font></b></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NBCUniversal Headquarters, Other and Eliminations include overhead and eliminations </font><font face="Arial">among</font><font face="Arial"> the NBCUniversal businesses. For the quarter ended </font><font face="Arial">June&nbsp;30</font><font face="Arial">, 201</font><font face="Arial">5</font><font face="Arial">, NBCUniversal Headquarters, Other and Eliminations operating cash flow loss was $</font><font face="Arial">167</font><font face="Arial"> million compared to a loss of $</font><font face="Arial">159</font><font face="Arial"> million in the </font><font face="Arial">second </font><font face="Arial">quarter of 201</font><font face="Arial">4.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, NBCUniversal Headquarters, Other and Eliminations operating cash flow loss was $309 million compared to a loss of $323 million in 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Corporate, Other and Eliminations</font></b></p>

<td width="7%" valign="top" style="border:none;border-top:solid #C9C9C9 1.5pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:7.5%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:8.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Corporate, Other and Eliminations </font><font face="Arial">primarily </font><font face="Arial">include corporate operations, Comcast-Spectacor and eliminations </font><font face="Arial">among</font><font face="Arial"> Comcast&#146;s businesses. For the quarter ended </font><font face="Arial">June&nbsp;30</font><font face="Arial">, 201</font><font face="Arial">5</font><font face="Arial">, Corporate, Other and Eliminations revenue was ($</font><font face="Arial">216</font><font face="Arial">) million compared to ($</font><font face="Arial">201</font><font face="Arial">) million in 201</font><font face="Arial">4</font><font face="Arial">. The operating cash flow loss was $</font><font face="Arial">244</font><font face="Arial"> million</font><font face="Arial">, including $79 million of transaction-related costs, </font><font face="Arial">compared to a loss of $</font><font face="Arial">194</font><font face="Arial"> million in the </font><font face="Arial">second </font><font face="Arial">quarter of 201</font><font face="Arial">4, which included $44 million of transaction-related costs.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, Corporate, Other and Eliminations revenue was ($397) million compared to ($426) million in 2014.&#160; The operating cash flow loss was $456 million, including $178 million of transaction-related costs, compared to a loss of $367 million in the first six months of 2014, which included $61 million of transaction-related costs.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Notes:</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1 We define Operating Cash Flow as operating income (loss) before depreciation and amortization, excluding impairment charges related to fixed and intangible assets and gains or losses on the sale of assets, if any.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2 Earnings per share amounts are presented on a diluted basis.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3 We define Free Cash Flow as Net Cash Provided by Operating Activities (as stated in our Consolidated Statement of Cash Flows) reduced by capital expenditures, cash paid for intangible assets</font><font face="Arial">, principal payments on capital leases</font><font face="Arial"> and cash distributions to noncontrolling interests; and adjusted for any payments and receipts related to certain nonoperating items, net of estimated tax benefits.</font><font face="Arial">&#160; The definition of Free Cash Flow excludes any impact from Economic Stimulus packages.&#160; These amounts have been excluded from Free Cash Flow to provide an appropriate comparison.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.35pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All percentages are calculated on whole numbers. </font><font face="Arial">Minor d</font><font face="Arial">ifferences may exist due to rounding.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:9.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Comcast Corporation</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:9.0pt;">Comcast Corporation (Nasdaq: CMCSA, CMCSK) is a global media and technology company with two primary businesses, Comcast Cable and NBCUniversal. Comcast Cable is the nation&#146;s largest video, high-speed Internet and phone provider to residential customers under the XFINITY brand and also provides these services to businesses. NBCUniversal operates news, entertainment and sports cable networks, the NBC and Telemundo broadcast networks, television production operations, television station groups, Universal Pictures and Universal Parks and Resorts. Visit </font><u><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:9.0pt;">www.comcastcorporation.com</font></u><font size="1" face="Arial" style="font-size:9.0pt;"> for more information.</font></p>

<DOCUMENT>
<TYPE>EX-99.2
<SEQUENCE>3
<FILENAME>a15-15979_1ex99d2.htm
<DESCRIPTION>EX-99.2
<TEXT>


<html>
<head>



  </head>
<body link=blue lang="EN-US">
<div>
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;99.2</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;99.2 &#150; Explanation of Non-GAAP and Other Financial Measures</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">This Exhibit&nbsp;99.2 to the accompanying Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K for Comcast Corporation (&#147;Company&#148;, &#147;we&#148;, &#147;us&#148; or &#147;our&#148;) sets forth the reasons we believe that presentation of financial measures not in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP) contained in the earnings press release filed as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 to the Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K provides useful information to investors regarding our financial condition and results of operations.&nbsp; To the extent material, this Exhibit&nbsp;also discloses the additional purposes, if any, for which our management uses these non-GAAP financial measures.&nbsp; A reconciliation of these non-GAAP financial measures with the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures is included in the earnings press release itself.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">Operating Cash Flow is the primary basis used to measure the operational strength and performance of our businesses. Free Cash Flow and Unlevered Free Cash Flow are additional performance measures used as indicators of our ability to service and repay debt, make investments and return capital to investors, through stock repurchases and dividends.&#160; We also adjust certain historical data on a pro forma basis following certain acquisitions or dispositions to enhance comparability.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">Operating Cash Flow is defined as operating income (loss) before depreciation and amortization, excluding impairment charges related to fixed and intangible assets and gains or losses on the sale of assets, if any. This measure eliminates the significant level of noncash depreciation and amortization expense that results from the capital-intensive nature of certain of our businesses and from intangible assets recognized in business combinations.&#160; It is also unaffected by our capital structure or investment activities. Our management and Board of Directors use this financial measure to evaluate our consolidated operating performance and the operating performance of our operating segments and to allocate resources and capital to our operating segments. It is also a significant performance measure in our annual incentive compensation programs.&#160; We believe that Operating Cash Flow is useful to investors because it is one of the bases for comparing our operating performance with that of other companies in our industries, although our measure of Operating Cash Flow may not be directly comparable to similar measures used by other companies.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">Because we use Operating Cash Flow to measure our segment profit or loss, we reconcile it to operating income, the most directly comparable financial measure calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP, in the business segment footnote to our quarterly and annual consolidated financial statements.&#160; Therefore, we believe our measure of Operating Cash Flow for our segments is not a &#147;non-GAAP financial measure&#148; as contemplated by Regulation G adopted by the Securities and Exchange Commission.&#160; Consolidated Operating Cash Flow is a non-GAAP financial measure.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">Free Cash Flow, which is a non-GAAP financial measure, is defined as &#147;Net Cash Provided by Operating Activities&#148; (as stated in our Consolidated Statement of Cash Flows) reduced by capital expenditures, cash paid for intangible assets, principal payments on capital leases and cash distributions to noncontrolling interests; and adjusted for any payments and receipts related to certain nonoperating items, net of estimated tax effects (such as income taxes on investment sales and nonrecurring payments related to income tax and litigation contingencies of acquired companies).&#160; Unlevered Free Cash Flow is Free Cash Flow before cash paid interest.&#160; We believe that Free Cash Flow and Unlevered Free Cash Flow are also useful to investors as the basis for comparing our performance and coverage ratios with other companies in our industries, although our measure of Free Cash Flow and Unlevered Free Cash Flow may not be directly comparable to similar measures used by other companies.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">Pro forma data is used by management to evaluate performance when certain acquisitions or dispositions occur.&#160; Historical data reflects results of acquired businesses only after the acquisition dates while pro forma data enhances comparability of financial information between periods by adjusting the data as if the acquisitions or dispositions occurred at the beginning of the preceding year.&#160; Our pro forma data is adjusted for the timing of acquisitions or dispositions, the effects of acquisition accounting, eliminating the costs and expenses directly related to the transaction, but does not include adjustments for costs related to integration activities, cost savings or synergies that have been or may be achieved by the combined businesses. We do not believe our pro forma data is a non-GAAP financial measure as contemplated by Regulation G.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">In certain circumstances we also present &#147;adjusted&#148; data, to exclude certain gains, losses or other charges, net of tax (such as from the sales of investments or dispositions of businesses).&#160; This &#147;adjusted&#148; data is a non-GAAP financial measure.&#160; We believe, among other things, that the &#147;adjusted&#148; data may help investors evaluate our ongoing operations and can assist in making meaningful period-over-period comparisons.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\108697\15-15979-1\task7496771\15979-1-mo.htm',USER='108697',CD='Jul 21 13:08 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;99.2 &#150; Explanation of Non-GAAP and Other Financial Measures, cont&#146;d</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">Non-GAAP financial measures should not be considered as substitutes for operating income (loss), net income (loss) attributable to Comcast Corporation, net cash provided by operating activities or other measures of performance or liquidity reported in accordance with GAAP.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">Additionally, in the opinion of management, our pro forma data is not necessarily indicative of future results or what our results would have been had the acquired businesses been operated by us after the assumed earlier date.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">In Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 to this Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K we provide reconciliations of Free Cash Flow in Table 4, Consolidated Operating Cash Flow in Table 1 and &#147;adjusted&#148; data in Tables 4 and 5.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.5pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
